| st_Chinese.ts | StDesignSettingDialog | Lossy Materials | 有损材料 |
| st_Chinese.ts | StDesignSettingDialog | This option will treat materials with electric or magnetic losses as dispersive materials and fit them using the Djordjevic-Sarkar model. As a result, the permittivity and conductivity of the materials will vary with the simulation frequency. If this option is not used, the permittivity and conductivity of the materials will remain constant and will not change with the simulation frequency. | 这个选项将有电损耗和磁损耗的材料视作色散材料，并使用Djordjevic-Sarkar进行拟合。并且，材料的相对介电常数和电导率可以随着仿真频率变化。如果没有使用这个选项，那材料的相对介电常数和电导率将会保持一个常数，并且不会跟着仿真频率变化。 |
